# CHANGELOG

All notable changes to Aisha CRM will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

---

## [Unreleased]

### Fixed

- **Finance Ops — Clear Test Data can now actually delete sandbox finance events (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/migrations/178_finance_audit_events_allow_test_delete.sql` (NEW)): `finance.audit_events` is append-only — migrations 173 + 175 install two BEFORE DELETE triggers that fire for EVERY row, so `clearFinanceTestData`'s `DELETE … WHERE is_test_data = true` always raised and sandbox finance data was never clearable. Migration 178 recreates the two audit_events delete triggers with a `WHEN (old.is_test_data is distinct from true)` guard — they fire (and block) ONLY for LIVE events; TEST events bypass them and are deletable. LIVE finance events remain strictly append-only; the shared trigger functions (still protecting journal_entries/journal_lines) are untouched. **Not applied** by merge — apply with 176/177 before relying on the finance Clear Test Data path.
- **Finance Ops — TEST adapter jobs are kept out of the provider worker (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`): the materializer wrote `finance.adapter_jobs` rows for TEST writes too, but that table has no `is_test_data` column and `adapterJobProcessor.claimPersistent` claims ANY queued row by tenant/status — so approving a TEST finance approval (with the adapter worker + provider writes enabled) could enqueue and process the sandbox job as a REAL provider write. `runPersistentWrite` now SKIPS materialization when `isTestData` is true (test jobs stay visible via the partitioned projection but never enter the claimable canonical table). Test added.
- **Finance Ops — mode switch aborts before persisting when the current mode is unreadable (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): if the pre-switch mode lookup threw, `previousMode` stayed null and a later failed rebuild's `failSwitch()` returned 503 WITHOUT reverting — leaving `/runtime/status` on the new mode while projections stayed on the old partition (the half-applied switch this guard exists to prevent). `applyFinanceDataModeChange` now throws `FINANCE_MODE_SWITCH_PRECHECK_FAILED` (503) BEFORE persisting when it can't read the current mode (nothing is changed). Test added: nothing persisted when the pre-switch read fails.
- **Finance Ops — unresolved Test/Live mode now FAILS CLOSED, not fail-safe-to-TEST (Codex PR #634 review round 2: 2×P1 + 1×P2)** (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`, `backend/workers/financeProjectionWorker.js`): the earlier fixes defaulted an unresolvable data mode to TEST, which Codex flagged as worse than failing — a Live write/poll guessed onto TEST corrupts the partition. Now fail-closed everywhere: (1) `runWrite` throws `FINANCE_DATA_MODE_UNRESOLVED` (503) instead of stamping the write `is_test_data=true` on a lookup error (a live write must not be persisted to the test partition, omitted from live reads and deletable by test cleanup); (2) the projection worker SKIPS a tenant's poll (records it failed, retries next cycle) instead of replaying an arbitrary partition into the shared projection rows. Tests updated: write → 503; worker skips the unresolvable tenant while a resolvable sibling still runs.
- **Finance Ops — a DEGRADED rebuild fails the mode switch too (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): the fail-loud switch only reverted on a _thrown_ rebuild; a `replayAll` that RESOLVED `{ outcome:'degraded' }` (shadow discarded, live store left on the old partition) still reported success. `applyFinanceDataModeChange` now treats a non-empty `degraded` result the same as a throw — reverts the persisted mode and returns 503 (shared `failSwitch` helper). Test added: a degraded rebuild reverts + throws.
- **Finance Ops — `/runtime/status` audit count partitioned by data mode (Codex PR #634 P2)** (`backend/lib/finance/readAdapters/pgAuditEventsReader.js`, `projectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter.js`, `backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): `pgAuditEventsReader.count` filtered only by tenant, so in TEST mode `counts.audit_events` / `persistence_lag.audit_events_total` included LIVE events even though `/audit-events` is filtered to TEST (misstating the dashboard). `count(tenantId, isTestData)` now partitions when given; `getRuntimeStatus(tenantId, { isTestData })` threads it; the route resolves the mode first and passes the active partition (PERSISTENT-only; `null`=all). Test added: the audit count is scoped to the active partition.
- **Finance Ops — projection worker replays only the active Test/Live partition (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/workers/financeProjectionWorker.js`): the background `finance-projection-worker` polled `eventStore.replay(tenantId)` with NO `isTestData` filter, so after a partitioned mode-switch rebuild the next poll re-projected BOTH partitions into the shared `projection_state` — undoing the isolation (e.g. switching to TEST with no test events would let the worker replay LIVE events into the test projections). `runProjectionPollCycle` now takes an injectable `resolveIsTestData(tenantId)` and replays `eventStore.replay(tenantId, isTestData)` for the tenant's ACTIVE partition; the production resolver (`defaultResolveIsTestData`) reads `fetchFinanceDataMode`. FAIL-SAFE to TEST when the mode can't be resolved (never replay live into test). With no resolver injected the filter is `null` (replay all — the back-compatible Slice-1 behavior). Tests (`financeProjectionWorker.test.js`, +3): per-tenant active partition, resolver-throws → test, no-resolver → null.
- **Finance Ops — in-memory mode refuses LIVE (no isolation to advertise) (Codex PR #634 P2)** (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): in non-persistent deployments `runWrite()` and the read adapter share ONE un-partitioned in-memory bucket, so switching TEST→LIVE would expose sandbox test entries through the live read endpoints. `applyFinanceDataModeChange` now throws `FINANCE_LIVE_REQUIRES_PERSISTENT` (409) when `!persistent && mode === 'live'` — BEFORE persisting — so an in-memory tenant stays test-only (the safe default); LIVE requires `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS` where the partitioning is real. The existing in-memory test was repointed to `test`; a new test asserts live is refused + not persisted.
- **Finance Ops — mode-switch rebuild failure is now actually fatal (Codex PR #634 P1)** (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`): the earlier fail-loud fix in `applyFinanceDataModeChange` only reverts + 503s when `rebuildFinanceProjections` throws — but `rebuildFinanceProjections` SWALLOWED a `replayAll` infra failure (logged + returned normally), so the switch still reported success with `projection_state` left on the old partition. `rebuildFinanceProjections` now RE-THROWS the `replayAll` failure so each caller owns the policy: the mode switch reverts the mode and returns 503 (no half-applied switch reported as success); `clearFinanceTestData` already wraps the call in try/catch and stays non-fatal (its delete already committed). Test flipped from "non-fatal/empty summary" to "re-throws" (`persistentWriteRunner.test.js`); the clear's non-fatal path stays green.
- **Finance Ops — "Create test entries" feedback no longer reads "Refreshing…" forever** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`, `src/components/finance/FinanceCreatePanel.jsx`, `src/pages/FinanceOps.jsx`): after a sandbox create succeeded the panel set `"Created sandbox entry. Refreshing…"` and never updated it, so it looked perpetually refreshing even though the entry was created and the counts had refreshed. Now the "Refreshing…" copy is transient — shown only while the refetch runs — and is replaced by a settled `"Created sandbox entry ✓ — check the tabs to review it."` once it completes. `FinanceOps.handleRefresh` now RETURNS the `fetchStatus()` promise so the panel actually awaits the refetch before settling (previously it fired-and-forgot). Test added (`FinanceCreatePanel.test.jsx`): the feedback settles to the "check the tabs" copy and no longer contains "Refreshing…". 17/17 finance create-panel + smoke tests green.
- **Finance Ops — Test/Live read segregation on the two raw event-stream endpoints (Codex P1)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`, `backend/routes/finance.v2.js`, `backend/lib/finance/financeDomainService.js`, `backend/lib/finance/auditEvidenceBuilder.js`): the Slice 6 partitioning was threaded into writes + projection rebuilds, but `GET /api/v2/finance/audit-events` and `GET /api/v2/finance/evidence-packs` read the durable event stream DIRECTLY (not via the rebuild that segregates the other reads), so in persistent mode a `live` tenant could still receive dormant `test` events and a `test` tenant could receive live events. Fixed by resolving the active mode at read time and threading an `is_test_data` filter into both paths: new route helper `resolveReadIsTestData(req)` (PERSISTENT-only — returns `null`/no-filter in in-memory mode where events are unstamped; FAIL-SAFE to TEST so an unresolved mode never exposes live events); `financeDomainService.listAuditEvents(tenantId, isTestData = null)` now passes `is_test_data` to `eventStore.query`; `buildEvidencePack(events, { …, isTestData = null })` threads it through `resolveEvents` into `.replay(tenantId, isTestData)` / `.query({ tenant_id, is_test_data })`. `null` = no filter everywhere (the store treats null/undefined as "all events"), so the array path and the in-memory default are byte-for-byte unchanged. Tests (`finance.v2.persistentWrites.test.js`, +3): test-mode `/audit-events` returns only test events (no live leak), live-mode returns only live (no test leak), and `/evidence-packs` counts only the active partition (2 test vs 1 live over the same stream).
- **Finance Ops — data-mode switch fails loud instead of silently serving the old partition (Codex P2)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`, `backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): `applyFinanceDataModeChange` previously persisted the new mode then SWALLOWED any post-switch projection-rebuild error and returned success. Because `projection_state` is shared per (projection, tenant), a failed rebuild left the OLD partition's rows in place — so reads kept serving the opposite partition while `/runtime/status` reported the new mode (a silent test↔live leak on switch failure). Now: on rebuild failure it REVERTS the persisted mode to the pre-switch value (captured via an injected `getFinanceDataMode`, so status stays consistent with the un-rebuilt projections) and THROWS `FINANCE_MODE_SWITCH_REBUILD_FAILED` (503) so the operator retries — never a silent success. The `PUT /settings/data-mode` handler passes `getFinanceDataMode` for the rollback. The unit test that locked the non-fatal behaviour was rewritten to assert the loud/revert path (+ a no-resolvable-previous-mode variant that still throws). Full finance backend suite 582/582.
- **Finance Ops — projection runner's replay sort also honors the PG `seq` (Codex PR #633 follow-up)** (`backend/lib/finance/projections/projectionRunner.js`): even with the store ordering by `(created_at, seq)`, the runner's `compareEvents` re-sorted replayed rows and tie-broke same-timestamp events only on the in-memory `_seq` — falling back to the random `id` UUID for Postgres rows (which carry `seq`, not `_seq`), discarding the store's append order inside every projection rebuild (hydrate's `runner.replay`). `compareEvents` now resolves a monotonic append index from `_seq` OR the PG `seq` column (`Number(seq)` — pg returns `bigint` as a string) before the id fallback. Test added: same-timestamp events with ascending `seq`/descending `id` replay in append order.
- **Finance Ops — persistent replay preserves append order (Codex PR #633)** (`backend/migrations/179_finance_audit_events_append_seq.sql` (NEW), `backend/lib/finance/financeEventStore.pg.js`): the Postgres event store ordered replay/query by `(created_at, id)`. `created_at` is the DB clock and `id` is a random UUID, so two events one command appends in the same instant tie on `created_at` and then order by UUID — NOT append order. e.g. `simulateDealWon` appends `draft_created` then `approval.requested`; if the approval's UUID sorted first, hydrate (`rebuildBucketFromEvents`) and the journal projection applied the pending snapshot before the draft, leaving the journal stuck as `draft`. Migration 179 adds a monotonic `seq bigint generated always as identity` column and re-keys the replay index to `(tenant_id, created_at, seq)`; the store now orders replay/query by `(created_at, seq)` — matching the in-memory store's `_seq` tie-break. `seq` is DB-assigned (the INSERT never writes it). **Not applied** by merge — apply before enabling persistent mode. Test flipped from "tie-break by id ASC" to "tie-break by APPEND order (seq)".
- **Finance Ops — reversal approvals now appear in the approval queue (Codex PR #634)** (`backend/lib/finance/projections/approvalQueueProjection.js`): `reverseJournalEntry` emits the reversal's pending approval ONLY inside `finance.journal.reversal_requested` (`payload.approval`), but the approval_queue projection consumed only the `finance.approval.*` lifecycle events. So in persistent mode the reversal approval was missing from `GET /approvals`, and approving its id replayed `finance.approval.approved` against an unknown record → degraded the projection. The projection now also consumes `finance.journal.reversal_requested` as a create-only request (handled identically to `finance.approval.requested`; both carry `payload.approval`). Test added: a reversal_requested creates a pending entry, then approving it resolves cleanly.
- **Finance Ops — `finance.adapter_jobs.id`/`aggregate_id` widened to `text` so materialized rows actually insert (Codex PR #633 P1)** (`backend/migrations/177_finance_adapter_jobs_text_ids.sql` (NEW), `backend/lib/finance/persistentAdapterJobWriter.js`): the domain service generates PREFIXED string IDs (`adapter_job_<uuid>`, `journal_<uuid>`), but `172_finance_ops_runtime_scaffold.sql` declared `finance.adapter_jobs.id` and `aggregate_id` as `uuid`. The Slice-2 materializer inserts those prefixed strings → Postgres rejects them (22P02) → the non-fatal catch swallows it → the write returns success and the projection shows a queued job, but no row lands in the table, so `adapterJobProcessor.claimPersistent` never has a runnable job. Migration 177 widens both columns to `text` (drops the uuid PK default; `tenant_id` stays `uuid`). **Not applied** by merging — apply before enabling the persistent adapter worker. The materializer carries a code note pointing at 177.
- **Finance Ops — capture events only after the durable append resolves (Codex PR #633 P1)** (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`): the capturing event store pushed each envelope into `captured` BEFORE awaiting `resolvedEventStore.append`, so if the durable append rejected, the (non-durable) envelope was still advanced into projections AND materialized into `finance.adapter_jobs` — letting the SQL adapter worker claim a job with no event-store fact. Now the envelope is captured only after the append RESOLVES; a rejected append captures nothing. Test added: a rejecting append → command throws, zero rebuilds, zero materializations.
- **Finance Ops — adapter-job reads surface `next_attempt_at` (Codex PR #633 P2)** (`backend/lib/finance/readAdapters/projectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter.js`): the projection now stores a retryable failure's backoff ETA on the queue item and the `/adapter-jobs` route serializes `j.next_attempt_at`, but `listAdapterJobs` dropped it, so `?status=queued` reported `next_attempt_at: null` for transient failures in persistent mode. Now copies `item.next_attempt_at` through. Test added: a transient `sync_failed` job reads back `queued` with its `next_attempt_at`.
- **Finance Ops — persistent writes now materialize `finance.adapter_jobs` rows so the worker can claim them (Codex PR #633 P1)** (`backend/lib/finance/persistentAdapterJobWriter.js` (NEW), `backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`, `backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): in persistent mode `runPersistentWrite` runs the command against a per-request IN-MEMORY domain service, so the in-memory `promoteLinkedAdapterJobs` path emitted `finance.adapter.sync_queued` and mutated the bucket but NOTHING ever inserted a `finance.adapter_jobs` row. The runtime adapter worker (`adapterJobProcessor.claimPersistent`) only drains `finance.adapter_jobs WHERE status = 'queued'`, so after `simulate/deal-won` + approve the job showed `queued` in `/adapter-jobs` (from the projection) but was never claimed or processed. Fixed with a new `materializeAdapterJobs({ pool, tenantId, events })` that UPSERTs `finance.adapter_jobs` from the captured adapter-job events (`approval.requested` draft + the three sync events), status derived from the event type (transient `sync_failed` ⇒ `queued`, permanent ⇒ `failed`; mirrors the projection), `ON CONFLICT (id)` idempotent, scoped to the write's tenant. Wired into `runPersistentWrite` after the durable append (best-effort, NON-FATAL — the events are durable and the projection already reflects the job); the route passes `adapterJobPool: pgPool`. Tests: new `persistentAdapterJobWriter.test.js` (8 — draft/queued/transient→queued/permanent→failed, tenant boundary, no-pool no-op, upsert-throws non-fatal) + `persistentWriteRunner.test.js` (+2 — materializer invoked with the captured `sync_queued`; skipped with no pool). Full finance backend suite 535/535.
- **Finance Ops — adapter-queue projection surfaces the real provider error (Codex PR #633 P2)** (`backend/lib/finance/projections/adapterQueueProjection.js`): for a real `finance.adapter.sync_failed`, the provider error is at `payload.error.message` (`buildSyncFailedEvent`), not on the `payload.adapter_job` snapshot (just `{ ...job, status: 'failed', … }`). The projection read `job.error_message`, so persistent `/adapter-jobs` returned `last_error: null` for every processor-emitted failure (only synthetic tests that put the error on the snapshot worked). Fixed by sourcing `error_message` from `payload.error.message` first, falling back to the snapshot field. Test added: a `sync_failed` with the error only on `payload.error.message` surfaces it.
- **Finance Ops — adapter-queue projection: transient sync failures stay `queued`, not `failed` (Codex PR #633 P2)** (`backend/lib/finance/projections/adapterQueueProjection.js`): the projection that backs persistent `/adapter-jobs` stamped every `finance.adapter.sync_failed` as terminal `failed`. But `runAdapterPollCycle` re-queues a TRANSIENT (retryable) failure — it writes the job row back to `status: 'queued'` with a `next_attempt_at` and emits NO follow-up `sync_queued` (the event carries the classification in `payload.permanent`). So a still-retryable job showed as `failed` in the API and was dropped from `/adapter-jobs?status=queued` until some later event. Fixed with a new `statusForEvent(event)` that projects a `sync_failed` with `payload.permanent === false` back to `queued` (only a PERMANENT failure is terminal; absent flag ⇒ terminal, the conservative back-compat default), and the queue item now carries the authoritative `next_attempt_at` (added to the stored record and `toQueueItem`, surfaced by the `/adapter-jobs` route which already mapped it). Tests (`adapterQueueProjection.test.js`, +3): transient ⇒ queued + `next_attempt_at`; permanent ⇒ failed; retries-exhausted transient→permanent moves queued→failed. Full finance backend suite 524/524.

### Added

- **Finance Ops — dormant test-data indicator + switch confirm (slice 6d)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`): the Finance Ops console now surfaces how much dormant TEST finance data exists for a tenant and asks for confirmation before a superadmin flips Test/Live.
  - **Route (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`)**: `GET /runtime/status` now attaches `data.test_data_count` — the count of the tenant's TEST finance events. New injectable resolver `opts.getTestDataCount({ tenantId, isTestData })` defaults to the persistent event store's partitioned `getCount(tenantId, true)`; the in-memory path has no durable test partition so it reports `0`. FAIL-SAFE: wrapped in try/catch, defaults to `0` on any error — never breaks `/runtime/status`.
  - **UI (`src/components/finance/RuntimeOverview.jsx`)**: new optional, backward-compatible prop `testDataCount = 0`. When `> 0`, renders a dormant indicator (`data-testid="runtime-overview-dormant-test"`, "⚠ N test record(s) exist for this tenant.") in ANY mode (so live mode still reminds you dormant test data exists). The Test/Live toggle now requests confirmation before switching when test data exists: clicking the target mode shows an inline confirm (`runtime-overview-switch-confirm`) with "Switch to {Mode}" (`-yes` → `onChangeMode(target)`) and "Cancel" (`-cancel` → dismiss). With `testDataCount === 0` the switch is immediate (no confirm). Component stays presentation-only.
  - **Page (`src/pages/FinanceOps.jsx`)**: passes `testDataCount={status?.test_data_count ?? 0}` to `<RuntimeOverview/>`.
  - Tests: `finance.v2.routes.test.js` (+ in-memory defaults to 0, injected count surfaced with `isTestData=true`, counter-throws fails safe to 0) and `RuntimeOverview.test.jsx` (+ indicator shown/hidden by count, confirm-on-switch with dormant data, yes/cancel behaviour, immediate switch at count 0). All existing RuntimeOverview + FinanceOps.smoke tests green (33 frontend); finance backend suite 578/578.

- **Finance Ops — wire finance into the per-tenant QA "Clear Test Data" button (slice 6c)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`): the QA console's "Clear Test Data" button (`POST /api/testing/cleanup-test-data`) now also clears a tenant's finance TEST events. Finance is event-sourced; the `is_test_data` partition (6a) on `finance.audit_events` separates Test from Live. The clear is PER-TENANT and best-effort — it NEVER fails the overall QA cleanup.
  - **New helper (`backend/lib/finance/clearFinanceTestData.js`)**: `clearFinanceTestData({ pool, getSupabaseClient, tenantId, logger, rebuild, eventStore, storeProvider })` — (1) `DELETE FROM finance.audit_events WHERE is_test_data = true AND tenant_id = $1 RETURNING id` (parameterized; capturing the deleted count); (2) resolves the tenant's CURRENT mode via `fetchFinanceDataMode` and REBUILDS the tenant's projections from that mode (`isTestData = mode === 'test'`) so the shared `projection_state` reads are correct after the clear (test ⇒ empties; live ⇒ unchanged). `tenantId` is REQUIRED (throws if absent). The rebuild is NON-FATAL (the delete already committed) — a throw is `logger.warn`'d and yields `rebuilt:false`. `getSupabaseClient`/`eventStore`/`storeProvider`/`rebuild` are injectable so the helper is fully unit-testable with spies (no real DB); real builders default when not injected. Returns `{ deleted, rebuilt }`.
  - **Wired into `backend/routes/testing.js`**: a finance pass added to the `cleanup-test-data` handler after the CRM-table deletions. Only when a `tenant_id` is provided (finance clear is per-tenant) it calls `clearFinanceTestData({ pool: _pgPool, getSupabaseClient, tenantId, logger })`, records `results['finance.audit_events'] = { deleted, rebuilt, success: true }`, and adds `deleted` to `totalDeleted`. Without a `tenant_id` it records `{ skipped: 'tenant_id required for finance clear' }` and touches nothing. An error records `{ deleted: 0, success: false, error }` and continues (never fails the whole cleanup).
  - Tests: new `backend/__tests__/lib/finance/clearFinanceTestData.test.js` (6 spy-driven cases — exact parameterized DELETE, isTestData test→true/live→false, thrown-rebuild non-fatal, thrown data-mode-fetch non-fatal, missing-tenantId throws) and `backend/__tests__/routes/testing.test.js` (+2 — handler invokes the finance clear for a tenant via a stub pool; skips when no tenant_id). UI (6d) is out of scope.

- **Finance Ops — rebuild projections on a data-mode SWITCH (slice 6b-2)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`): closes the read-staleness gap after a superadmin flips a tenant's Test/Live mode. The shared `projection_state` row per (projection, tenant) holds the CURRENT mode's projection; until 6b-2 it kept the OLD mode's data until the next write, so a read right after a switch showed stale (other-mode) data. Now, on a successful switch, every registered finance projection is rebuilt from the NEW mode's events so reads immediately reflect the new mode. PERSISTENT-only (in-memory mode has no persistent projections → no-op) and NON-FATAL (the mode is already persisted; a rebuild error is logged, never fails the switch; degraded projections already fail-closed via `FinanceReadDegradedError` on read).
  - **Rebuild helper (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`)**: new exported `rebuildFinanceProjections({ eventStore, storeProvider, workers, createRunner, tenantId, isTestData, logger })` — validates `eventStore`/`storeProvider`/`tenantId`, builds the default five-worker runner (injectable), then `runner.replayAll(tenantId, isTestData)` rebuilds EVERY projection from the new mode's partition. A degraded projection or a throwing `replayAll` is `logger.warn`'d (tenant + projection) and NON-FATAL; returns `{ rebuilt: [...], degraded: [...] }`. Does NOT change the projection-store keying or the read adapter.
  - **Route (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`)**: extracted exported `applyFinanceDataModeChange({ tenantId, mode, persistent, setFinanceDataMode, rebuildFinanceProjections, eventStore, storeProvider, logger })` keeps the `PUT /settings/data-mode` handler thin and unit-testable WITHOUT going through `validateTenantAccess`'s superadmin Supabase lookup: it persists then (persistent + stores present) rebuilds from the NEW mode (`isTestData = mode === 'test'`), swallowing rebuild errors. The handler now delegates to it; `rebuildFinanceProjections` is injectable via `opts`. Response unchanged (`{ status:'success', data:{ mode } }`).
  - Tests: `persistentWriteRunner.test.js` (+5 — `replayAll(tenantId, isTestData)` threading test→true/live→false, degraded + throwing replayAll are non-fatal, required-arg validation) and `finance.v2.routes.test.js` (+5 `applyFinanceDataModeChange` — persist-then-rebuild order, isTestData test→true/live→false, in-memory skips rebuild, missing-stores skips, rebuild error swallowed). Existing 403-forbidden setter route test kept green. Full backend finance suite 570/570.

- **Finance Ops — Test/Live data-mode threaded into the projection REBUILD on the write path (slice 6b-1)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`): the persistent write path's ADVANCE step now rebuilds each affected projection from the ACTIVE mode's events only, so a test-mode write rebuilds projections from the test partition and a live-mode write from the live partition. Builds on 6a (which threaded the mode through HYDRATE + envelope stamping). The shared `projection_state` row per (projection, tenant) always holds the current mode's projection; a mode SWITCH-triggered rebuild is deferred to 6b-2.
  - **Projection runner (`backend/lib/finance/projections/projectionRunner.js`)**: `replay(projectionName, tenantId, isTestData = null)` and `replayAll(tenantId, isTestData = null)` thread the mode through `doReplay(worker, tenantId, isTestData)` → `eventStore.replay(tenantId, isTestData)`. `isTestData = null` is fully backward-compatible (no filter = all events); `dispatch` and the projection-store keying are unchanged.
  - **Persistent write runner (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`)**: the ADVANCE loop now calls `runner.replay(projectionName, tenantId, isTestData)` (the `isTestData` option already existed on `runPersistentWrite` from 6a), so the rebuilt projection reflects only the current mode's events.
  - **Route (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`)**: `runWrite(req, command)` resolves the tenant's active data mode via the existing `getFinanceDataMode({ tenantId, req })` and passes `isTestData` into `runPersistentWriteFn`. FAIL-SAFE to TEST: a mode-lookup error defaults `isTestData = true` so a lookup failure never silently writes/rebuilds over live data. Default (in-memory) branch unchanged.
  - Tests: `projectionRunner.test.js` (+4 spy-store cases proving the mode tuple is forwarded), `persistentWriteRunner.test.js` (rebuild now asserts the third arg), and `finance.v2.persistentWrites.test.js` — the app builder injects `getFinanceDataMode` (defaults `'live'`), and a NEW write-side segregation test proves a test-mode write can approve a TEST approval (200) but a LIVE approval is invisible (404). Full backend finance suite 560/560.

- **Finance Ops — Test/Live data-mode partition on the EVENT layer (slice 6a)** (`feat/finance-test-live-data-mode`): adds an `is_test_data` boolean partition flag to the finance event stream so Test and Live data can be cleanly separated. Events now carry the flag, the write path stamps every appended envelope with the tenant's current mode, and the persistent write path's hydrate-replay loads only the current mode's events. Everything defaults to `is_test_data=false` (Live) so existing behaviour is byte-for-byte preserved. (Projection rebuild + read-path partitioning land in a later sub-slice; this slice does NOT touch the projection store, runner, read adapter, or routes.)
  - **Migration `backend/migrations/176_finance_is_test_data_partition.sql`** (new, authored only — not applied): `ALTER TABLE finance.audit_events ADD COLUMN is_test_data boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false`; drops the replay index `idx_finance_audit_events_replay` from migration 173 (`tenant_id, created_at, id`) and recreates it as `(tenant_id, is_test_data, created_at, id)` so mode is a leading filter for replay.
  - **Event envelope (`backend/lib/finance/financeEventEnvelope.js`)**: `createFinanceEventEnvelope({ ..., isTestData = false })` now includes `is_test_data` in the returned object.
  - **PG event store (`backend/lib/finance/financeEventStore.pg.js`)**: `is_test_data` added to `INSERT_COLUMNS` (defaults `false`); `replay(tenant_id, isTestData = null)`, `query({ ..., is_test_data })`, and `getCount(tenant_id, isTestData = null)` add a parameterized `is_test_data` filter only when provided — `null`/`undefined` returns all events (unchanged).
  - **In-memory event store (`backend/lib/finance/financeEventStore.js`)**: `append` preserves `is_test_data` (defaults `false`); `replay`/`query`/`getCount` mirror the PG store's optional mode filter.
  - **Persistent write runner (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`)**: `runPersistentWrite({ ..., isTestData = false })` replays the current mode's partition on hydrate (`replay(tenantId, isTestData)`) and stamps every captured/appended envelope with `is_test_data: isTestData`. The ADVANCE step is unchanged (deferred to 6b).
  - Tests: extended `financeEventStore.pg.test.js`, `financeEventStore.test.js`, `persistentWriteRunner.test.js`, and new `financeEventEnvelope.test.js`. Full backend finance suite 555/555.

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1 persistent reads + writes migration: `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS=true` is now fully durable end-to-end** (`feat/finance-ops-phase4-1-persistent-reads-migration`). Persistent mode now MOUNTS and is fully functional — durable reads, durable writes, and read-your-write — closing the divergence flagged by Codex PR #632 P1 `#3344750464`. This consolidates the migration's slices:
  - **Invoice projection (`finance.projection.invoices`)** — consumes `finance.invoice.draft_created` / `draft_updated` and returns full invoice snapshots (mirrors `journalEntriesProjection`), registered in the runner, read-adapter workers, worker deployment, and replay harness; `getRuntimeStatus` now wires the real invoice-projection count (previously hardcoded `0`).
  - **Read-adapter methods (`listInvoices` / `listApprovals` / `listAdapterJobs`, Task 3)** on BOTH adapters, so the 4 remaining service-backed reads (`/draft-invoices`, `/approvals`, `/adapter-jobs`, and `/journal-drafts`) route through projections in persistent mode. `InMemoryFinanceReadAdapter` delegates to the domain service; `ProjectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter` reconstructs the same record shape per-request from the `invoices`, `approval_queue`, and `adapter_queue` projections (fresh `createStoreProvider()` each call). Lossless-projection fix: `approvalQueueProjection.js`'s `toResolvedEntry` now additively carries `requested_by` / `requested_at` so resolved approvals keep the requester + request timestamp on `/approvals?status=all`. New `backend/__tests__/lib/finance/readAdapters/readAdapterParity.test.js` asserts InMemory vs ProjectionBacked agree field-by-field on the route-consumed fields.
  - **Persistent write orchestration (Task 8, activation capstone)** — the 6 mutating endpoints (`POST /draft-invoices`, `PATCH /draft-invoices/:id`, `POST /journal-drafts`, `POST /simulate/deal-won`, `POST /journal-entries/:id/reverse`, `POST /approvals/:id/approve`) now run through `persistentWriteRunner.runPersistentWrite({...})` in persistent mode: it hydrates the domain bucket from the durable event stream (so a durable-only approval is found, not 404'd), runs the same service command with identical args, and synchronously advances the shared projections so the write is visible to the very next read (read-your-write). The read path and write path share ONE projection-store provider and ONE persistent event store, built once at construction (`createStoreProvider` threaded into `defaultFinanceReadAdapterFactory`; `runPersistentWrite` injectable). Default (in-memory) behaviour is byte-for-byte unchanged; `buildSource().mode` reports `'persistent'` vs `'in_memory'` per the deploy-time flag. New acceptance suite `backend/__tests__/routes/finance.v2.persistentWrites.test.js`: (A) approving a durable-only approval returns 200 (bucket hydration), (B) a POSTed journal draft is immediately visible via GET (synchronous advancement / read-your-write). (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`)

### Changed

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1 Task 8b: `adapter_queue` projection materializes DRAFT adapter jobs** (`feat/finance-ops-phase4-1-persistent-reads-migration`): closes the persistent-mode parity gap where un-synced draft adapter jobs were omitted from `/adapter-jobs` and the runtime `adapter_jobs` count. `simulateDealWon` creates an adapter job with `status: 'draft'` and carries it in the `finance.approval.requested` payload as `adapter_job`, but the `adapter_queue` projection only consumed the three `finance.adapter.sync_*` events, so a draft never materialized until a `sync_queued` was emitted. **Fix** (`backend/lib/finance/projections/adapterQueueProjection.js`): `finance.approval.requested` is now a consumed event; when its payload carries an `adapter_job` (GUARD — historical/non-draft approval.requested events without one are skipped, never degraded) the projection upserts it keyed by `adapter_job_id` with status `'draft'`, and `getProjection` returns a new `draft` bucket (`{ draft, queued, running, failed, completed }`). Because records are keyed by id and re-bucketed by current status at read time, a later `sync_queued` for the same id cleanly transitions the job draft→queued with no duplicate left in `draft`. The upsert is set-by-id, so the new path is idempotent under double-apply (verified by `projectionDoubleApply.test.js`). Downstream: `projectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter.js` `listAdapterJobs` now concatenates the `draft` bucket and `countReadModel` sums it, so persistent `/adapter-jobs` and the runtime count include drafts — matching the in-memory domain service. `readAdapterParity.test.js`'s adapter-jobs comparison upgraded from a deliberate subset to FULL set equality on the route-consumed fields. Tests: `adapterQueueProjection.test.js` (+3 draft cases), `adapterQueueProjection.integration.test.js` (draft-bucket + clean-transition assertions), `projectionDoubleApply.test.js` (+draft idempotency proof).

### Fixed

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1: boot guard removed (persistent mode activated); durable mutations wired** (`feat/finance-ops-phase4-1-persistent-reads-migration`): the boot guard added in PR #632 (which made `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS=true` refuse to mount the finance v2 routes until reads + writes were durable) is now REMOVED in `createFinanceV2Routes` — the durable read/write surface above makes the gate obsolete. The fail-closed no-pool / no-stores guard is kept (persistent mode still requires a Postgres pool). Mount tests in `finance.v2.routes.test.js` flipped: persistent + pool now MOUNTS; no-pool still refuses. Only `backend/routes/finance.v2.js` + tests changed for the activation; the domain service, projections, and `persistentWriteRunner.js` are untouched.

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1: persistent-write advance CATCHES UP affected projections by rebuild (read-your-write robust to lag)** (`feat/finance-ops-phase4-1-persistent-reads-migration`): `runPersistentWrite`'s ADVANCE step previously dispatched ONLY the new envelopes a write appended onto the in-process projections. But a projection can be BEHIND the durable event stream (cold start, async-worker lag, or — the core scenario — approving an approval whose `finance.approval.requested` is durably in the event store but was never projected into this process). Dispatching `finance.approval.approved` onto an `approval_queue` projection that lacks the prior `pending` entry made the worker throw and DEGRADED the projection. **Fix** (`backend/lib/finance/persistentWriteRunner.js`): the advance now computes the DISTINCT set of affected projection names (every worker whose `consumedEvents` includes any captured envelope's `event_type`) and `runner.replay(projectionName, tenantId)` each one — REBUILDING it from `eventStore.replay(tenantId)` (which now includes this write's appended events) into a shadow store that is atomically promoted. Rebuild is idempotent, recovers a degraded projection, and is correct regardless of prior state. Advancement stays strictly NON-FATAL: a `degraded` outcome or a thrown `replay` (infra/PG) is logged via `logger.warn` and the loop continues; the command result (or error) is still returned/rethrown. Tradeoff documented: rebuild is O(stream) per affected projection per write — acceptable for the low-write-volume finance console (incremental catch-up-since-cursor can optimize later). Also extracted a single `runWrite(req, command)` helper in `backend/routes/finance.v2.js`, replacing the identical persistent/in-memory branch repeated across all 6 mutating handlers (behaviour unchanged). Tests: `persistentWriteRunner.test.js` reworked to assert the rebuilt affected-projection set; the acceptance suite proves a post-approve `GET /approvals?status=all` returns the approval as `approved` with `decided_by` set (caught up, not degraded). Full backend finance suite 520/520.

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1: atomic finance writes (append-before-mutate) (Codex PR #632 follow-up P2)**: with the persistent-events route lift, the in-memory domain service is wired to the Postgres event store, but every write method mutated its in-memory bucket **before** awaiting `eventStore.append()`. A failed/timed-out append left the bucket changed while the persistent store recorded nothing — the still-service-backed read endpoints (`/draft-invoices`, `/journal-drafts`, `/approvals`, `/adapter-jobs`, …) would then expose a phantom draft/approval/job, and the service's duplicate/state guards would diverge from the durable log. **Fix:** every write flow now appends the event first and mutates the in-memory bucket only after the append resolves — `createDraftInvoice`, `updateDraftInvoice`, `createJournalDraft`, `simulateDealWon` (single `approval.requested` gate before promoting the draft + creating the approval + queuing the adapter job), `reverseJournalEntry`, `approveFinanceAction`, and the in-memory branch of `adapterJobPromoter` (`financeDomainService.js`, `adapterJobPromoter.js`). The duplicate-approval guard is split into `assertNoDuplicateApproval()` (pre-append, so no event is persisted for a duplicate) + `pushApproval()` (atomic re-check at push). New tests: `financeDomainService.atomicWrites.test.js` (6 flows) + a promoter in-memory case — each asserts a failing event store leaves the read surface phantom-free. Full backend finance suite 480/480.
- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1 persistent-path correctness (Codex PR #632 review: 3×P1 + 1×P2)**: makes the persistent path actually correct, not just reachable. (1) `pgAuditEventsReader.js` now queries the schema-qualified `finance.audit_events` (was bare `audit_events`, which would 503 under the default search_path). (2) **Slice #1 write path**: in persistent mode `createFinanceV2Routes` builds the domain service with the Postgres event store (`createFinancePgEventStore`), so mutating endpoints write to `finance.audit_events` instead of the in-memory bucket — previously persistent reads (Postgres projections) and writes (in-memory) were split-brain. (3) `ProjectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter` now builds a **fresh projection-store provider per request** (`createStoreProvider`), so reads reflect the latest worker-persisted `projection_state` rather than a snapshot cached for the router lifetime. (4) Hardened the `getState` regression-test stub to a projection-store-shaped fake (array `keys()`). New tests: `pgAuditEventsReader.test.js`, persistent-write-path route test, fresh-provider-per-request test. Full backend finance suite 473/473.
- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1 P2: `getRuntimeStatus` projection_state read failures now fail-closed** (`backend/lib/finance/readAdapters/projectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter.js`): The per-projection lag/status loop in `getRuntimeStatus()` was wrapping `storeProvider.getState(...)` in a try/catch that collapsed any error to `state = null` (lines 117-122), returning `200` with `cursor: null` / `is_degraded: false` output instead of the promised degraded `503`. This weakened the §6 no-silent-fallback contract (design doc lines 52, 175, 217) specifically for runtime-status, which operators use to detect projection health. **Fix:** `getState` failures now raise `FinanceReadDegradedError` the same way `getLiveStore` and `audit_events` failures already do. New test added: `backend/__tests__/lib/finance/readAdapters/projectionBackedFinanceReadAdapter.test.js` (test 6). All 22 finance tests green (16 route tests + 6 adapter tests). Codex review: Slack TS `1780422309.136489`.

### Added

- **Finance Ops — Phase 4-1 persistent-events route lift (T5–T8)** (`feat/finance-ops-phase4-1-route-lift`): wires the projection-backed read path into the Finance v2 routes, completing the slice whose read subsystem (the `journal_entries` projection, `InMemory`/`ProjectionBacked` read adapters, `accountingEngine` from-ledger derivation, and the `finance.approval.requested` enrichment — T0–T4) landed on `main` via #631. `backend/routes/finance.v2.js` now selects a `FinanceReadAdapter` **once at construction time** (single env read; no per-request read, no runtime swap — persistence mode is deploy-time) and routes all 5 GETs through it. The old unconditional split-brain throw is **replaced** by a loud-on-misconfig guard inside `defaultFinanceReadAdapterFactory`: `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS=true` without a Postgres pool refuses to mount — the fail-closed posture preserved structurally. Adds `backend/lib/finance/readAdapters/pgAuditEventsReader.js`. The default posture (flag false/unset) is byte-for-byte unchanged — the in-memory branch behaves identically via `InMemoryFinanceReadAdapter`. No silent fallback: projection/audit read failures surface as 503 (`FinanceReadDegradedError`), never in-memory data. Tests: `finance.v2.adapterSelection.test.js` (selection / loud-on-misconfig / deploy-time), route-suite parity (in-memory branch unchanged), no-endpoint-expansion guard (§9 row 10). Design amendment §4.1 + implementation plan added. **Flag stays false; durability remains operator-gated (design §10) — no migration, no env flip, no staging/prod action.**

### Changed

- **Replace in-stack Ollama with AI Cloud Server** (`docker-compose.yml`, Doppler): removed the `aishacrm-ollama` container (CPU-based `llama3.2:3b`/`qwen2.5-coder:3b`) and replaced with vLLM running Qwen2.5-14B-AWQ on the HP Omen 35L (RTX 5070 Ti) AI cloud server. `LOCAL_LLM_BASE_URL`, `LOCAL_LLM_API_KEY`, `LOCAL_LLM_MODEL`, and `SUMMARY_LLM_MODEL` are now sourced from Doppler (all three envs updated). The `ollama_data` volume and `depends_on: ollama` were removed from the backend service. No application logic changed; the `local` provider path uses the same env vars.

### Security

- **P0 security hardening — tenant/authz, CSRF, secrets/logging pass**:
  - `backend/server.js`: Added `authenticateRequest` + `requireSuperAdminRole` to `/api/tenants` mount -- previously had no auth at all, allowing unauthenticated callers to cascade-delete entire tenants. Added `authenticateRequest` to `/api/users` and `/api/permissions` mounts -- individual `requireAuth`/`requireAdminRole` guards in those routers were being bypassed because `req.user` was never populated.
  - `backend/routes/users.js`: Added `requireAdminRole` to `POST /bulk-delete` and `DELETE /:id`. Added `requireSuperAdminRole` to `POST /admin-password-reset`. Added `requireAdminRole` to `POST /generate-recovery-link`.
  - `backend/middleware/authenticate.js`: Removed unconditional `logger.warn` that fired on every request, flooding logs. Gated behind `AUTH_DEBUG=true` at debug level.
  - `backend/__tests__/routes/p0-security.test.js`: 21 new tests covering all hardened routes. All pass.

### Added

- **Finance Ops — beta CSV exports** (`feat/finance-ops-beta-exports`): read-only CSV export for recordkeeping handoff on the Finance Ops panels (Draft Invoices, Journal Drafts, Approvals, Adapter Queue, Journal Entries, Audit Timeline, Ledger Summary, Evidence pack). New `src/components/finance/financeCsv.js` (`columnsToRecords`/`recordsToCsv`/`financeExportFilename`/`downloadCsv`) serializes each export from the panel's **displayed column model** (header = column label, cell = `render(row) ?? row[key]`) so the CSV matches what users see; Ledger Summary exports operator labels + `$` amounts (not raw `*_cents`/JSON). New `FinanceCsvExportButton.jsx` is disabled with an operator-facing tooltip when a panel is empty. Exports cover the displayed page (50-row default; documented limitation), are tenant-scoped + read-only (no new endpoint, no mutation), and carry no secrets/credentials (`/adapters` is not exported; evidence export is metadata + integrity hashes only, asserted by test). **PDF export deferred** (follow-up). Tests: `financeCsv.test.js`, `FinanceCsvExportButton.test.jsx`, and per-panel `*.export.test.jsx`. Docs: checklist §5 → Implemented, limitations updated, `docs/architecture/finance/finance-ops-beta-exports-slice-design.md`, `docs/plans/2026-05-31-finance-ops-beta-exports.md`.

New parity tests lock the source of truth at every layer: `backend/__tests__/lib/finance/accountingEngine.integrity.test.js` (hand-computed ledger/P&L/balance-sheet totals against a multi-status fixture; proves `draft`/`pending_approval` entries are excluded from the ledger) and an "engine parity" block in `backend/__tests__/routes/finance.v2.read-routes.test.js` (the `/ledger` `/profit-loss` `/balance-sheet` route bodies equal `accountingEngine` output bit-for-bit). New `src/components/finance/__tests__/LedgerSummary.integrity.test.jsx` asserts the rendered currency figures equal the source numbers. New docs `docs/architecture/finance/finance-ops-beta-integrity-checklist.md` (4 principles → enforcement → evidence, Implemented/Partial/Deferred) and `docs/architecture/finance/finance-ops-beta-limitations.md` (honest deferrals: in-memory persistence, runtime.mode placeholder, projection cursors, persistent-events route lift, provider writes, CSV/PDF export). Design + plan: `docs/architecture/finance/finance-ops-beta-integrity-slice-design.md`, `docs/plans/2026-05-31-finance-ops-beta-integrity.md`.

### Changed

- **Finance Ops — Ledger Summary balance state is now three-valued** (`src/components/finance/LedgerSummary.jsx`): the balance-sheet "Balanced" row previously defaulted to "Yes" whenever `is_balanced` was absent (`is_balanced !== false`), which could mask a calculation or load error. It now shows **Yes** only on an explicit `is_balanced === true`, a visible amber **"No — unbalanced (ledger integrity issue)"** warning on `false`, and **Unknown** when the field is absent; a failed balance-sheet fetch surfaces the existing per-section error and renders no balance row at all. Satisfies the beta blocker "empty states must not hide calculation errors." Read-only preserved; no backend/contract change.

### Fixed

- **Finance Ops — Ledger Summary operator-friendly rendering (UI-1D P2 regression closed on the Read API branch)** (`src/components/finance/LedgerSummary.jsx` + `src/components/finance/__tests__/LedgerSummary.test.jsx`): Andrei's dev-container validation of Finance Read API Slice 1 showed the Ledger Summary tab still dumping raw API field shapes (`accounts []`, `totals {"debit_cents":0,...}`, `net_income_cents`, `is_balanced`) with the copy "Field shapes are forwarded as-is." **Root cause:** the operator-friendly Ledger Summary polish was authored as the Codex UI-1D P2 fix on `feat/finance-ops-ux-preview` (commit `7deb03ac`) and was never merged to `main`; the Read API implementation branch was cut from `main` (`13312d1d`), which only carries the raw-shape UI-1C baseline from `c1b94d28` (#618). It was **not** a rewire by the Read API slice — that commit (`442f0a4d`) never touched `LedgerSummary.jsx`. **Fix:** ported the already-Codex-cleared polished component + strengthened test verbatim from `7deb03ac` onto this branch (no reinvention, no drift). The panel now formats integer cents as USD currency with readable labels (Debits/Credits, Revenue/Expenses/Net income, Assets/Liabilities/Equity, Balanced Yes/No), renders per-section operator empty states ("No ledger accounts available for this tenant yet.", etc.), and no longer surfaces raw `*_cents` keys or JSON as the operator view. The strengthened test asserts currency formatting AND that raw keys (`debit_cents`, `net_income_cents`, `is_balanced`) are not rendered — it fails against the raw-shape component and passes against the polished one. Read-only preserved (only the Refresh control; no mutating affordance). Frontend finance suite 92/92.

- **Finance UI Slice 1 — Read-only API gaps design freeze: Codex P1/P1/P2 fixes** (`docs/architecture/finance/finance-ui-slice-1-api-gaps-design.md`, Codex re-review of the local UI-1D worktree, Slack TS `1780111337.893189`): Applied the 3 findings; doc-only, no runtime/contract change to backend code. **P1 — `/adapter-jobs` (§6.4) dropped canonical adapter-job states.** The frozen `status` filter and row enum were `queued|succeeded|failed`, but the canonical in-memory source creates jobs in `draft` (`backend/lib/finance/financeDomainService.js:504-517`, `status: 'draft'`) and `projection-contracts.md` §7 + its Design Decisions note make `draft` and `running` canonical statuses. **Fix:** row `status` enum and `?status=` filter widened to the canonical migration-172 set `draft|queued|running|succeeded|failed` (+`all`), plus a "Status vocabulary" bullet reconciling the row-level status with the `adapterQueueProjection` bucket vocabulary (`queued/running/failed/completed`, `completed ← succeeded`) so no canonical state is dropped. **P1 — `/evidence-packs` (§6.8) specified a historical metadata list with no honest source of truth.** The only backing runtime, `backend/lib/finance/auditEvidenceBuilder.js`, exports just `queryAuditTimeline` / `getReversalChain` / `buildEvidencePack` — a pure on-demand pack builder, not a persistent pack registry; the frozen contract invented `pack_type` / `title` / `generated_at` / `summary` / `artifact_count` list rows. **Fix:** §6.8 re-specified as an honest on-demand single-pack build (`?from=&to=&target_id=` mapping to `buildEvidencePack`) returning the freshly built pack's `pack_id` / `generated_at` (= this request's build time) / `scope` / `summary` / `artifact_count` / integrity hashes, with `total` and pagination removed; the §4 inventory, §7 blocked-on-4-1 table, §10 empty-state test note, and §14 out-of-scope (persistent pack registry + per-id retrieval deferred to a future slice) updated to match. **P2 — `/adapters` (§6.7) overstated ERPNext sandbox capability.** The example advertised `push_final`, but the adapter is `mode: 'draft_only'` and `pushFinal` throws `AdapterCapabilityError` (`backend/lib/finance/accountingAdapters/erpnextSandboxAdapter.js:336-340`). **Fix:** `capabilities` reduced to the operations the adapter actually implements (`push_draft`, `sync_status`, `reconcile` — `:283,343,373`), added `mode: "draft_only"` and an explicit `unsupported: ["push_final"]`, dropped the unbacked `pull_status`, and added an honest-capability-disclosure bullet citing the adapter source. No backend semantic change, no client wrapper, no migration, no env-var flip; all 16 Phase 3-13 §7 guardrails preserved.

### Added

- **Finance Ops RBAC & Access Matrix design freeze (Track E)** (`docs/architecture/finance/finance-ops-rbac-access-matrix.md` (NEW)): Design / documentation only — no code change, no backend route mounted, no env-var change, no migration. Companion to Slice 1 §11.3 (access posture), Phase 4-1 (persistent-events route lift), and the Track C operator copy guide. Single source of truth for the Finance Ops access model. **§4 role taxonomy** — six roles (superadmin, tenant admin, finance admin/operator, finance viewer, non-finance user, dev-mode mock superadmin) with data-model identification, expected behaviour at every layer (process mount, `validateTenantAccess`, per-tenant `financeOps` module gate, frontend nav visibility, page render, future write actions), and Implemented-today vs Deferred with file:line citations for every Implemented claim. **§5 module gating interactions** — the `financeOps` Module Settings toggle + `requireAdminRole` mutation auth, canonical-wins resolution between `financeOps` and the legacy `enterpriseFinance` alias, the alias-aware auto-seed/backfill rule, and the dev-only enablement path (no production shortcut). **§6 the matrix** — a role × surface table where every cell is `Impl` / `Impl on-branch` / `Defer` / `N/A` with the gate (or absence) that justifies it; the six write routes that already exist (`finance.v2.js:492-580` — create/update draft invoice, create journal draft, simulate deal-won, reverse, approve) are labelled **Impl with no role gate** (reachable by any enrolled-tenant caller, no role differentiation — a finance-admin/viewer split must retrofit a route check onto them), while reject/replay/adapter-retry/cancel/provider-sync are **Defer (no route)** across all roles. **§7 frontend↔backend parity rules** — no frontend role gate that diverges from backend (Slice 1 §11.3); "mirror everything, enforce nothing in the mirror." **§8 deferred items + binding rule** — any new role gate MUST land at the backend route layer first, then the frontend mirror, never frontend-only. **§9/§11** guardrails + posture. No env-var flip, no migration, no provider write, no staging/Coolify/Doppler mutation, no production action; canonical-wins gate logic preserved. (Recovered Track E deliverable — authored on `main` HEAD `13312d1d`, landed via its own PR; baseline since reconciled to HEAD `34e7c0a`. Per Codex review on the PR: corrected the matrix to show the six finance write routes already exist with no role gate (above); separated the `ENABLE_FINANCE_OPS` 404 mount gate from the `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS` boot-time split-brain `throw` in §3; reconciled all formerly "Impl on-branch" cells/prose to **Impl** now that the `feat/finance-ops-ux-preview` UI/nav/seed work merged via #624 (`4487acec`); and corrected the `crm_access` precondition from `Impl` to **`FE-only`** with a new §7.6 — it is enforced only in the frontend (`permissions.js:306`), the backend stack never inspects `crm_access`, so a `crm_access:false` user can still call `/api/v2/finance/*` directly — including the six existing write routes, not reads only (fail-closed mirror divergence); and generalized §7.6 to also cover explicit per-user `navigation_permissions['FinanceOps'] === false` (`permissions.js:417`) — likewise a frontend-only view gate the backend never reads (distinct from the admin-gated `navigation_permissions` **edit** routes), with the tenant-selected nav-visibility matrix row carrying the same `FE-only` caveat; added the seven shipped Slice 1 read endpoints (#623 — `GET /draft-invoices` `:239`, `/journal-drafts` `:269`, `/approvals` `:302`, `/adapter-jobs` `:332`, `/audit-events` `:362`, `/adapters` `:427`, `/evidence-packs` `:455`) as their own matrix rows so the read surface is complete; and corrected the two `navigation_permissions` **edit** rows that overstated enforcement — the **tenant-default** edit is `Defer` (footnote ³: the UI's `Tenant.update({settings:{default_navigation_permissions}})` is silently discarded — `PUT /api/tenants/:id` only persists `branding_settings` and the `tenant` table has no `settings` column), and the **per-user** edit is `Impl, ungated` (footnote ⁴: `PUT /api/users/:id` persists `navigation_permissions`/`nav_permissions` but `/api/users` is mounted at `server.js:379` with no `authenticateRequest`/`requireAdminRole` — a security gap flagged for follow-up).)

- **Finance Read API — Implementation Slice 1** (branch `feat/finance-ops-read-api-implementation-slice1`): Implemented the read-only Finance Ops GET endpoints frozen in `finance-ui-slice-1-api-gaps-design.md` §6, wired the matching frontend client helpers, and replaced the UI gap cards with live read views. **Read-only end-to-end — no mutation, no provider writes, no env flips, no migration, no staging/prod action; all 16 Phase 3-13 §7 guardrails preserved.** **Implemented (7):** `GET /api/v2/finance/{draft-invoices, journal-drafts, approvals, adapter-jobs, audit-events, adapters, evidence-packs}`. **Deferred (1):** `GET /projection/cursors` — depends on the persistent projection store (kept as the only remaining `FINANCE_API_GAPS` read-endpoint gap; not faked). **Backend** (`backend/routes/finance.v2.js`): 7 GET handlers added inside the existing 3-gate stack (process `ENABLE_FINANCE_OPS` mount → `validateTenantAccess` → per-tenant `financeOps` module gate); reuse the `{status,data}` success / `{status,message,code,details}` error envelopes; every payload carries the §5.7 `data.source` provenance block (`mode:'in_memory'`); offset/limit clamped per §5.3 (never 400); `/audit-events` is cursor-paginated with an opaque tenant-scoped base64url cursor that rejects malformed AND cross-tenant cursors with `400 PAGINATION_INVALID`; `/evidence-packs` is an on-demand single-pack build via `auditEvidenceBuilder.buildEvidencePack` (metadata + integrity hashes only — no list/total/pagination); `sendError` extended to forward `code`/`details`. New module `backend/lib/finance/financeAdapterRegistry.js` provides the read-only declarative adapter metadata for `/adapters` (capability/status/posture discovery only — **no adapter instantiation, no credentials, no network, no write/sync/retry path**; `provider_writes_enabled` mirrors `FINANCE_PROVIDER_WRITES_ENABLED`, default false). `financeDomainService.js` gained pure read accessors `listInvoices` / `listAdapterJobs` and test seams `seedInvoice` / `seedAdapterJob` (additive, read-only). **Frontend** (`src/api/finance.js`): added GET wrappers `getDraftInvoices` / `getJournalDrafts` / `getApprovals` / `getAdapterJobs` / `getAuditEvents` / `getAdapters` / `getEvidencePack` (+ a `withQuery` helper) and removed the 7 retired `FINANCE_API_GAPS` entries (2 remain: `projectionCursors`, `runtimeMode`). **UI** (`src/components/finance/`): new reusable read-only `FinanceTablePanel`; rewired `DraftInvoicesPanel` / `JournalDraftsPanel` / `ApprovalQueuePanel` / `AdapterQueuePanel` / `AuditTimelinePanel` (cursor "Load more") / `SandboxAdapterPanel` (live adapter metadata, gap card removed) / `EvidencePlaceholder` (on-demand pack metadata) from gap cards to live views — read-only (only Refresh / Load more controls; no approve/reject/retry/cancel/generate/sync affordance); `ProjectionStatusPanel` keeps its gap card. **Documented §6 field-mapping deviations** (forced by the in-memory source; §5.7 `data.source` is the honesty signal): `amount_cents←total_cents`, `customer_name←null`, journal `aggregate_id←id` / `account_code←null` / `amount_cents←Σdebit_cents`, approval `subject_*←target_*` / `decided_*←approved_*`, adapter `attempts/next_attempt_at/last_error←0/null/null`, audit `occurred_at←created_at` / `actor←actor_id`, evidence `artifact_count←event_count`; `/adapters` adds `production_allowed:false` and a config-derived `status` that mirrors the worker's full registration gate (`financeAdapterWorker.js:484-516`): `not_registered` when the `FINANCE_ERPNEXT_*` creds are absent, `configuration_invalid` when present but the base URL fails the sandbox guard (the shared, now-exported `isSandboxBaseUrl` validator — same check the adapter constructor uses at `erpnextSandboxAdapter.js:162`), `registered` only when creds present AND the URL is sandbox-valid; `credentials_resolved` mirrors credential presence. **Tests:** `backend/__tests__/routes/finance.v2.read-routes.test.js` (44 — auth matrix, tenant isolation, shape parity, pagination clamping, cursor round-trip + malformed/cross-tenant rejection, journal-drafts⊆journal-entries invariant, no-mutation, `/adapters` no-credential/no-write assertions); updated `src/api/__tests__/finance.test.js` (wrapper URL/query/exports + 2-gap registry); new `src/components/finance/__tests__/LiveDataPanels.test.jsx`; updated `PartialAndGapPanels.test.jsx` / `GapStateCard.test.jsx` / `FinanceOps.smoke.test.jsx`. Backend finance suite 56/56, frontend finance suite 92/92.

}` error envelope + offset/limit OR cursor pagination conventions + 200-with-empty-array empty-state rule + `data.source.{mode,served_at,projection,cursor_lag_ms}` provenance disclosure + the 503 PROJECTION_DEGRADED contract — so per-endpoint sections only call out deviations. §6 specifies each endpoint individually: path + source-of-truth today (in-memory domain service / adapter runtime / audit-evidence builder) + source-of-truth after Phase 4-1 (persistent projection, named per endpoint) + request shape + response shape + empty state + pagination + cross-endpoint visibility rule (e.g. identifies which endpoints' persistent branches are blocked on Phase 4-1 (six of eight) vs. which are not (`/adapters`, `/evidence-packs`). §8 restates the Phase 4-1 no-silent-fallback contract so this packet does not weaken it: when persistent mode is on and the projection is degraded, the route returns 503, never falls back to in-memory. §9 binds the three-gate authorisation stack (process-level `ENABLE_FINANCE_OPS`, `validateTenantAccess`, per-tenant `financeOps` module gate with canonical-wins alias resolution) and explicitly states no route-level role gate is added (Slice 1 §11.3 carry-forward — any future role gate lands at the backend route first, then the frontend mirror). §10 enumerates the required test surface before any of these routes may mount: authorisation matrix (404 / 401 / 403 / 200 across `ENABLE_FINANCE_OPS` off, missing auth, cross-tenant, disabled-canonical, alias-only-enabled (canonical-wins alias path), disabled-canonical-with-enabled-alias (canonical-wins denial), and enabled-canonical), tenant isolation, response shape parity, pagination clamping + cursor cross-tenant rejection, empty-state correctness, no-mutation-surface assertion, plus the persistent-mode bit-parity + no-silent-fallback tests gated on Phase 4-1 landing. §11 enumerates the staging proof required before any production consideration. §12 restates every hard constraint. §13 acceptance + §14 explicit out-of-scope list (mutating endpoints, approve/reject/reverse/replay/retry/cancel/provider-sync UI, evidence-pack content retrieval, projection admin affordances, finance-admin vs finance-viewer role split, `ENABLE_FINANCE_PERSISTENT_EVENTS` / `FINANCE_PROVIDER_WRITES_ENABLED` activation). No backend semantic change, no client wrapper added, no mutation affordance, no env-var change, no migration, no provider write, no staging / Coolify / Doppler mutation, no production action; all 16 Phase 3-13 §7 safety guardrails preserved end-to-end. - **Finance Ops UI-1D — Codex P1: alias-aware auto-seed (no legacy-tenant clobber)** (`backend/routes/tenants.js`, `backend/scripts/debug/backfill-module-settings.js`, `src/components/shared/ModuleManager.jsx`, `backend/__tests__/routes/tenants.defaultModules.test.js`, `src/components/shared/__tests__/ModuleManager.financeOps.test.jsx`): Closes a critical regression introduced by the access-enablement entry below — when a tenant was enrolled via the legacy `enterpriseFinance` alias, both the `ModuleManager` auto-create-on-Settings-load path and `backfill-module-settings.js` treated the canonical `financeOps` key as missing and inserted a fresh `financeOps` row at `is_enabled:false`, which silently revoked access via canonical-wins (`backend/lib/finance/financeModuleGate.js:40-48`, `src/utils/permissions.js:362-378`). Fix: extracted alias-aware helpers — backend `selectMissingDefaultRows()` + `MODULESETTINGS_ALIASES = { financeOps: ['enterpriseFinance'] }` (exported from `tenants.js`); frontend `computeMissingModules()` (exported from `ModuleManager.jsx`) using `MODULE_ALIASES` from `navigationConfig.js` — both treat the presence of EITHER the canonical key OR any registered alias as "module already configured", so no disabled canonical row is inserted that would override an alias-enabled tenant. `getModuleStatus` also made alias-aware so the toggle correctly shows ON for an alias-enrolled tenant (was misleadingly OFF). New tests on both helpers prove the alias-present-only case is no longer treated as missing, the canonical-present case is still detected, and non-aliased modules remain correctly missing when absent. No backend semantic change, no mutation controls, no env/migration/provider/staging/production action; canonical-wins resolution in the module gate is preserved (we just stop creating the conflicting row).

- **Finance Ops UI-1D — access/enablement: Module Settings toggle + tenant seeding + nav visibility** (`src/components/shared/ModuleManager.jsx`, `backend/routes/tenants.js`, `src/utils/permissions.js`, `src/utils/__tests__/permissions.financeOps.test.js`, `src/components/shared/__tests__/ModuleManager.financeOps.test.jsx`, `backend/__tests__/routes/tenants.defaultModules.test.js`, `backend/scripts/debug/backfill-module-settings.js`, `src/components/settings/UserFormWizard.jsx`, `src/components/settings/NavigationPermissions.jsx`, `src/components/settings/TenantNavigationDefaults.jsx`, `src/components/settings/__tests__/NavigationPermissions.financeOps.test.jsx`, `docs/architecture/finance/finance-ux-preview-usability-test-plan.md`): Closes the dev-container access gap Andrei found — the Finance Ops page told users to enable `financeOps` in Module Settings, but there was no UI to do so and new tenants never got the row. **Frontend** — `ModuleManager` now has a "Finance Operations" entry plus a new `moduleKey` concept (`moduleKeyOf()`): most modules store their display name as `modulesettings.module_name` (legacy convention), but Finance Ops stores the canonical backend key `financeOps` the gate/nav/permissions expect, so a toggle can't write the wrong key. It defaults **disabled** (`defaultEnabled: false`) and auto-create + `getModuleStatus` honor that default, keeping the per-tenant gate meaningful (controlled rollout). The toggle reuses the existing admin-gated `/api/modulesettings` write — no new endpoint, no gate bypass. **Backend** — `tenants.js` adds `DEFAULT_DISABLED_MODULES = ['financeOps']` and a pure `buildDefaultModuleRows(tenantId)` so every new tenant is seeded a `financeOps` row at `is_enabled: false` (other defaults unchanged, still enabled); `DEFAULT_MODULES` + the builder are now exported for testing. **Tests (anti-drift, per Andrei's request)** — backend node:test asserts financeOps seeds disabled with the canonical key and no duplicates; a frontend vitest asserts the `ModuleManager` entry's `moduleKey` equals `navigationConfig.moduleMapping.FinanceOps` (`'financeOps'`) and is never the `enterpriseFinance` alias; extended `permissions.financeOps.test.js` locks superadmin + `crm_access` semantics — superadmin sees the page in global view but still respects a **disabled** per-tenant `financeOps` row when a tenant is selected (no bypass), enabling the row is what grants access, and `crm_access:false` is denied. **Codex P1 (nav visibility)** — enabling the module row alone didn't surface FinanceOps for users relying on role defaults, because `hasPageAccess()` fell through to `getDefaultNavigationPermissions()` which omitted `FinanceOps`; added `FinanceOps: true` to all four role-default tables in `src/utils/permissions.js` (still gated by the per-tenant module row — design §11.3, no frontend role gate that diverges from the backend), with new tests covering default-permission superadmin/admin/manager/employee. **Codex P3 (drift)** — `backfill-module-settings.js` now imports `buildDefaultModuleRows()` from `tenants.js` (single source of truth) instead of its own hardcoded list, so existing-tenant backfill includes `financeOps` (disabled) and can't drift. **Per-user + tenant permission editors** — `FinanceOps` was also absent from the per-user permission catalogs, so admins had no toggle to grant/revoke Finance Operations for a user. The **active** create/edit form is `UserFormWizard.jsx` (rendered by `EnhancedUserManagement`); its `NAV_MODULES` list (mapped into the wizard's Navigation step) and `DEFAULT_NAV_PERMISSIONS` both omitted Finance, so the toggle never rendered — added `FinanceOps` to both (`DEFAULT_NAV_PERMISSIONS.FinanceOps: true`, so it persists rather than being silently dropped on save; actual access still gated by the per-tenant `financeOps` module row). Also added it to the secondary editors `NavigationPermissions.jsx` (`ORDER` fallback, which renders because `User.schema()` is undefined) and the tenant-default editor `TenantNavigationDefaults.jsx` (`NAV_ITEMS`, `moduleName: 'financeOps'` so it cross-references the module row). Anti-drift test (`NavigationPermissions.financeOps.test.jsx`) asserts FinanceOps presence in all three catalogs + canonical-key parity. (`EnhancedUserManagement`'s legacy `UserFormModal.navigationPages` is dead code — never rendered — so left untouched.) **No** Finance v2 mutation controls/helpers, no provider writes, no env flips (`ENABLE_FINANCE_OPS` master switch unchanged), no migration application, no staging/Coolify/Doppler change, no production action; seeding affects only future tenant creation and does not mutate existing rows.
